# AI-Ready Lesson Prompts

Use these blocks to prompt Claude or Gemini for lesson narrative generation.

---

## Lesson 1 Prompt Block

```
LESSON 1 - 15 CHARACTERS

Characters to weave into narrative:
- 一 (yī, tone 1): "one" — A single proud line stands alone, singing "Yeeee!" - this is number one!
- 二 (èr, tone 4): "two" — Two parallel lines stack up, yelling "ERR!" when you count twice!
- 三 (sān, tone 1): "three" — Three horizontal lines rise like stairs, singing "Saaaan-shine" in harmony!
- 四 (sì, tone 4): "four" — Inside the box, your four items command "See this!" sharply!
- 五 (wǔ, tone 3): "five" — Five strokes converge at the crossing point, calling out "Woo"!
- 六 (liù, tone 4): "six" — A lid over eight yells "Leo!" for six sharp reasons!
- 七 (qī, tone 1): "seven" — Seven kids drew slashes across the night sky with bright sparklers, yelling "Chee!"!
- 八 (bā, tone 1): "eight" — Eight paths diverge like spreading wings, calling "Baaaa!" as they separate!
- 九 (jiǔ, tone 3): "nine" — Nine hooks around like a curving tail, bending as it says "Jiu"!
- 十 (shí, tone 2): "ten" — A cross at ten keeps asking "Shi? Why ten?" curiously!
- 口 (kǒu, tone 3): "Mouth" — Your mouth forms a perfect square, speaking "Ko" clearly spoken through parted lips!
- 日 (rì, tone 4): "Day" — The sun yells "REE!" sharply to wake you each day!
- 月 (yuè, tone 4): "Month" — The crescent moon marks time's passage, whispering "Yue!" as each month turns!
- 田 (tián, tone 2): "Rice Field" — In the rice field, farmers ask "Tian? Why so muddy?" curiously!
- 目 (mù, tone 4): "Eye" — Your eye angrily yells "MOO!" when dust gets in it!

Task: Create a cohesive lesson narrative that weaves all 15 characters
into an epic story. Each character should appear naturally in the narrative, with its
meaning reinforced through context. Include pinyin sound cues where possible.
```

---

## Lesson 2 Prompt Block

```
LESSON 2 - 16 CHARACTERS

Characters to weave into narrative:
- 古 (gǔ, tone 3): "ancient" — The stone takes the shape of ancient, calling out "Gu" - a vivid image to remember!
- 胡 (hú, tone 2): "recklessly" — A reckless fool with wild whiskers asks "Who? Hu?" questioning everything!
- 吾 (wú, tone 2): "I (literary)" — "I," says the mouth, questioning "Wu? Am I important?" with a sigh!
- 朋 (péng, tone 2): "Companion" — Two moons ask "Peng? Why are we companions?" questioning their friendship!
- 明 (míng, tone 2): "bright" — The sun and moon together question "Ming? Why so bright?" curiously!
- 唱 (chàng, tone 4): "to sing" — With your mouth, you command the sun to sing "Chang!" sharply!
- 晶 (jīng, tone 1): "sparkling" — Three suns sparkle cheerfully, singing "Jing!" high and happy!
- 品 (pǐn, tone 3): "Goods" — Three mouths bend down, drooping as they inspect goods saying "Pin"!
- 昌 (chāng, tone 1): "prosperous" — Two suns rise high, singing "Chang!" to celebrate prosperity!
- 早 (zǎo, tone 3): "early" — The morning sun still hangs low at dawn's early hour, yawning "Zao"!
- 旭 (xù, tone 4): "Rising Sun" — See how the sun forms rising sun? It shouts "Shu!" sharply as sunlight streams across the sky!
- 世 (shì, tone 4): "Generation" — Three tens stack up, yelling "Shi!" for each generation sharply!
- 胃 (wèi, tone 4): "Stomach" — Your stomach with a field inside yells "Way!" angrily when hungry!
- 旦 (dàn, tone 4): "Daybreak" — At daybreak, the sun commands "Dan!" sharply above the horizon!
- 凹 (āo, tone 1): "concave" — The strokes unite to show concave, singing "Aaooo!" cheerfully!
- 凸 (tū, tone 1): "convex" — The stick stands for convex, singing "Too!" cheerfully - a vivid image to remember!

Task: Create a cohesive lesson narrative that weaves all 16 characters
into an epic story. Each character should appear naturally in the narrative, with its
meaning reinforced through context. Include pinyin sound cues where possible.
```

## Lesson 3 Prompt Block

```
LESSON 3 - 18 CHARACTERS

Characters to weave into narrative:
- 自 (zì, tone 4): "oneself" — A nose points to oneself, yelling "Zi!" sharply with pride!
- 白 (bái, tone 2): "white" — The white sun asks "Bai? Why so bright?" questioning curiously!
- 百 (bǎi, tone 3): "hundred" — The white sun shines over a single line - one hundred times, calling "Bai"!
- 皂 (zào, tone 4): "Soap" — The white stands for soap, shouting "Zao!" sharply - a vivid image to remember!
- 中 (zhōng, tone 1): "Middle" — An arrow pierces straight through the middle, striking "Zhong!" at the bull's-eye!
- 千 (qiān, tone 1): "thousand" — A thousand people sing "Chian!" cheerfully marching together!
- 舌 (shé, tone 2): "Tongue" — Your tongue in your mouth asks "She? Why taste this?" questioning!
- 升 (shēng, tone 1): "Liter" — A liter rises up cheerfully singing "Sheng!" to the top!
- 昇 (shēng, tone 1): "to rise up" — The sun rises high, happily singing "Sheng!" at dawn!
- 丸 (wán, tone 2): "Pill" — A round pill asks "Wan? Why swallow me?" questioning curiously!
- 卜 (bǔ, tone 3): "Divination" — See how the stick forms divination? It whispers "Bu" softly!
- 占 (zhàn, tone 4): "to tell fortunes" — Your mouth commands the divination sharply "Zhan! Tell my fortune!"
- 上 (shàng, tone 4): "above" — Above the line, an arrow yells "Shang!" pointing up sharply!
- 下 (xià, tone 4): "below" — Below the line, an arrow commands "Xia!" pointing down sharply!
- 卡 (kǎ, tone 3): "Card" — A card bends and dips between above and below saying "Ka"!
- 卓 (zhuó, tone 2): "eminent" — An eminent person stands above, questioning "Zhuo? Am I tall enough?" curiously!
- 朝 (cháo, tone 2): "Dynasty" — The dynasty sun and moon question "Chao? Why our reign?" curiously!
- 嘲 (cháo, tone 2): "to ridicule" — The mouth ridicules, questioning "Chao? You call that a dynasty?" mockingly!

Task: Create a cohesive lesson narrative that weaves all 18 characters
into an epic story. Each character should appear naturally in the narrative, with its
meaning reinforced through context. Include pinyin sound cues where possible.
```

## Lesson 4 Prompt Block

```
LESSON 4 - 18 CHARACTERS

Characters to weave into narrative:
- 只 (zhǐ, tone 3): "only" — Like a mouth, this character means only and whispers "Zhi" spoken through parted lips!
- 貝 (bèi, tone 4): "Shellfish" — With a shellfish combined with a shell, you get shellfish - "Bay!" rings out sharply!
- 貼 (tiē, tone 1): "to paste" — When the stick meets the shellfish, they form to paste, singing "Tieh!" cheerfully!
- 貞 (zhēn, tone 1): "chaste" — The shellfish stands for chaste, singing "Zhen!" cheerfully!
- 員 (yuán, tone 2): "Employee" — Your employee shellfish asks "Yuan? Where's my paycheck?" questioning!
- 見 (jiàn, tone 4): "to see" — Eyes on legs command "Jian! See this!" sharply!
- 元 (yuán, tone 2): "Beginning" — At the beginning, two legs question "Yuan? Why start here?" curiously!
- 頁 (yè, tone 4): "Page" — The page head yells "Yeh!" sharply when turned!
- 頑 (wán, tone 2): "stubborn" — A stubborn head questions "Wan? Why should I?" refusing to budge!
- 凡 (fán, tone 2): "ordinary" — An ordinary table sighs "Fan? Why so plain?" questioning its fate!
- 肌 (jī, tone 1): "Muscle" — Muscles sing "Jee!" cheerfully when flexing happily!
- 負 (fù, tone 4): "defeated" — The shell takes the shape of defeated, shouting "Fu!" sharply!
- 勻 (yún, tone 2): "uniform" — An striking symbol for uniform that asks "Yun? Why equal?" curiously!
- 句 (jù, tone 4): "Sentence" — The mouth takes the shape of sentence, shouting "Ju!" sharply!
- 旬 (xún, tone 2): "Decameron" — Ten days question "Shun? Already a decameron?" asking where time went!
- 勺 (sháo, tone 2): "Ladle" — The ladle asks "Shao? Why scoop this?" questioning curiously!
- 的 (de, tone 5): "Bull's Eye" — The white ladle hits the bull's eye, saying "duh" neutrally!
- 首 (shǒu, tone 3): "Heads" — Picture heads taking form - it whispers "Sho" with vivid energy!

Task: Create a cohesive lesson narrative that weaves all 18 characters
into an epic story. Each character should appear naturally in the narrative, with its
meaning reinforced through context. Include pinyin sound cues where possible.
```

## Lesson 5 Prompt Block

```
LESSON 5 - 23 CHARACTERS

Characters to weave into narrative:
- 直 (zhí, tone 2): "straight" — Like an eye, this character means straight and asks "Zhi? Why so direct?"!
- 置 (zhì, tone 4): "to set up" — Set up the net straight, commanding "Zhi!" sharply in place!
- 具 (jù, tone 4): "Tool" — The crowded tool table had eyes painted on everything - juice boxes included!
- 真 (zhēn, tone 1): "true" — Ten eyes sing "Zhen!" happily seeing the truth!
- 工 (gōng, tone 1): "the Work" — The construction workers sang "Gong!" as they lifted the beams.
- 左 (zuǒ, tone 3): "Left" — The hand stands for left, whispering "Zuo" softly reached by outstretched fingers!
- 右 (yòu, tone 4): "Right" — Picture a mouth beside a hand: that's right, shouting "Yo!" sharply!
- 有 (yǒu, tone 3): "to possess" — To possess the moon with your right hand, it bends drooping saying "Yo"!
- 賄 (huì, tone 4): "bribe" — A bribe of shellfish yells "Hway!" sharply with each corrupt hand!
- 貢 (gòng, tone 4): "Tribute" — Tribute of work and shellfish commands "Gong!" sharply to the emperor!
- 項 (xiàng, tone 4): "Item" — The item page of your head yells "Shyang!" sharply!
- 刀 (dāo, tone 1): "Sword" — See how the sword forms sword? It sings "Dao!" cheerfully - a vivid image to remember!
- 刃 (rèn, tone 4): "Blade" — A dot on the blade yells "Ren!" sharply at the edge!
- 切 (qiè, tone 4): "to cut" — Cut with one sword, commanding "Chieh!" sharply!
- 召 (zhào, tone 4): "to summon" — Summon with your mouth and sword, yelling "Zhao!" sharply!
- 昭 (zhāo, tone 1): "evident" — See how the sun forms evident? It sings "Zhao!" cheerfully as sunlight streams across the sky!
- 則 (zé, tone 2): "Rule" — The rule with shellfish and sword questions "Zeh? Why obey?" curiously!
- 副 (fù, tone 4): "vice-" — The vice stands beside with a sword, commanding "Fu!" sharply!
- 丁 (dīng, tone 1): "fourth" — See how the nail forms fourth? It sings "Ding!" cheerfully - a vivid image to remember!
- 叮 (dīng, tone 1): "to sting" — When the nail meets the mouth, they form to sting, singing "Ding!" cheerfully!
- 可 (kě, tone 3): "can" — You can use your mouth bent down drooping saying "Kuh"!
- 哥 (gē, tone 1): "Older Brother" — This character represents older brother, singing "Guh!" cheerfully!
- 頂 (dǐng, tone 3): "crest" — Picture crest taking form - it whispers "Ding" with vivid energy!

Task: Create a cohesive lesson narrative that weaves all 23 characters
into an epic story. Each character should appear naturally in the narrative, with its
meaning reinforced through context. Include pinyin sound cues where possible.
```

- 孔 (kǒng, tone 3): "cavity" — This character represents cavity, whispering "Kong" softly - a vivid image to remember!
- 吼 (hǒu, tone 3): "to roar" — See how the mouth forms to roar? It whispers "Ho!" softly spoken through parted lips!
- 了 (le, tone 5): "-ed" — Completed action of child says "luh" neutrally when done!
- 女 (nǚ, tone 3): "Woman" — A striking symbol for woman that whispers "Nyu" softly - a vivid image to remember!
- 好 (hǎo, tone 3): "good" — A woman and child bend down drooping together, good and saying "Hao"!
- 如 (rú, tone 2): "to be like" — A woman's mouth asks "Ru? Are we alike?" questioning similarity!
- 母 (mǔ, tone 3): "Mother" — A striking symbol for mother that whispers "Mu" softly - a vivid image to remember!
- 貫 (guàn, tone 4): "to pierce" — Pierce through the shell sharply commanding "Guan!" with mother above!
- 兄 (xiōng, tone 1): "Elder Brother" — The strokes unite to show elder brother, singing "Shyong!" cheerfully!

Task: Create a cohesive lesson narrative that weaves all 12 characters

## Lesson 7 Prompt Block

```
LESSON 7 - 20 CHARACTERS

Characters to weave into narrative:
- 小 (xiǎo, tone 3): "small" — The person stands for small, whispering "Shyao" softly - a vivid image to remember!
- 少 (shǎo, tone 3): "few" — Picture few taking form - it whispers "Shao" with vivid energy!
- 吵 (chǎo, tone 3): "noisy" — The mouth takes the shape of noisy, whispering "Chao" softly!
- 大 (dà, tone 4): "large" — Like a person, this character means large and shouts "Da!" - a vivid image to remember!
- 尖 (jiān, tone 1): "tip" — The tip where small meets large sings "Jian!" cheerfully and sharp!
- 夕 (xī, tone 1): "Evening" — Like a moon, this character means evening and sings "Shee!"!
- 多 (duó, tone 2): "many" — The strokes unite to show many, asking "Duo? Why so many nights?" curiously!
- 夠 (gòu, tone 4): "enough" — Picture enough taking form - it shouts "Go!" with vivid energy!
- 外 (wài, tone 4): "outside" — Outside the evening divination yells "Why!" sharply beyond!
- 名 (míng, tone 2): "a Name" — Like a mouth, this character means a name and asks "Ming? Who am I?"!
- 厚 (hòu, tone 4): "thick" — Picture thick taking form - it shouts "Ho!" with vivid energy!
- 石 (shí, tone 2): "stone" — A stone at the cliff asks "Shi? How hard?" questioning curiously!
- 砂 (shā, tone 1): "Gravel" — This character represents gravel, singing "Sha!" cheerfully!
- 妙 (miào, tone 4): "wonderful" — Picture wonderful taking form - it shouts "Miao!" with vivid energy!
- 肖 (xiào, tone 4): "to resemble" — A striking symbol for to resemble that shouts "Shyao!" sharply!
- 削 (xiāo, tone 1): "to peel" — She used a knife to peel the apple, removing small bits at a time.
- 光 (guāng, tone 1): "ray" — See how the fire forms ray? It sings "Gwang!" cheerfully with flickering flames dancing high!
- 太 (tài, tone 4): "overly" — See how the dot forms overly? It shouts "Tai!" sharply - a vivid image to remember!
- 省 (shěng, tone 3): "to economize" — The eye stands for to economize, whispering "Sheng" softly - a vivid image to remember!
- 奇 (qí, tone 2): "strange" — A strange large person questions "Chi? Why so odd?" curiously!

Task: Create a cohesive lesson narrative that weaves all 20 characters
into an epic story. Each character should appear naturally in the narrative, with its
meaning reinforced through context. Include pinyin sound cues where possible.
```

## Lesson 8 Prompt Block

```
LESSON 8 - 46 CHARACTERS

Characters to weave into narrative:
- 川 (chuān, tone 1): "Stream" — A stream flows cheerfully singing "Chuan!" in three happy channels!
- 州 (zhōu, tone 1): "a state" — Picture a state taking form - it sings "Joe!" with vivid energy!
- 順 (shùn, tone 4): "to obey" — To obey, the stream flows by the page, commanding "Shun!" sharply!
- 水 (shuǐ, tone 3): "Water" — Like water, this character means water and whispers "Shway"!
- 永 (yǒng, tone 3): "Eternity" — Like water, this character means eternity and whispers "Yong"!
- 求 (qiú, tone 2): "to request" — Like water, this character means to request and asks "Chyo? May I have some?"!
- 泉 (quán, tone 2): "a Spring" — A spring of white water questions "Chuan? Where does it come from?" curiously!
- 原 (yuán, tone 2): "flatlands" — See how the white forms flatlands? It asks "Yuan? Why so flat?" curiously!
- 願 (yuàn, tone 4): "a wish" — An striking symbol for a wish that shouts "Yuan! Grant it!" sharply!
- 沖 (chōng, tone 1): "to wash away" — To wash away, water sings "Chong!" cheerfully rinsing middle!
- 泳 (yǒng, tone 3): "to swim" — See how the water forms to swim? It whispers "Yong" softly like ripples spreading across a pond!
- 洲 (zhōu, tone 1): "Continent" — A continent with water and state sings "Joe!" cheerfully and large!
- 沼 (zhǎo, tone 3): "Marsh" — The water stands for marsh, whispering "Zhao" softly like ripples spreading across a pond!
- 沙 (shā, tone 1): "Sand" — The water stands for sand, singing "Sha!" cheerfully like ripples spreading across a pond!
- 江 (jiāng, tone 1): "Yangtze" — The Yangtze water flows cheerfully singing "Jiang!" through the work!
- 汁 (zhī, tone 1): "Juice" — "Gee!" he said, extracting juice from ten oranges using water pressure.
- 潮 (cháo, tone 2): "Tide" — The tide of dynasty water questions "Chao? Why rise and fall?" curiously!
- 源 (yuán, tone 2): "source" — The source of water flatlands questions "Yuan? Where does it begin?" curiously!
- 活 (huó, tone 2): "lively" — The water and tongue unite to create lively, asking "Huo? Why so active?" curiously!
- 消 (xiāo, tone 1): "to extinguish" — The moon faded away as dawn extinguished the night.
- 況 (kuàng, tone 4): "Situation" — The situation of water mouth yells "Kwang!" sharply describing!
- 河 (hé, tone 2): "river" — When the river meets the mouth, they form river, asking "Huh? Why flow here?" curiously!
- 湖 (hú, tone 2): "lake" — A lake of water questions "Who? Hu?" curiously like reckless whiskers!
- 測 (cè, tone 4): "to fathom" — Like water, this character means to fathom and shouts "Tsuh!"!
- 土 (tǔ, tone 3): "Soil" — The soil takes the shape of soil, whispering "Too" softly - a vivid image to remember!
- 均 (jūn, tone 1): "to equal" — See how the soil forms to equal? It sings "June!" cheerfully!
- 肚 (du, tone 5): "belly" — A belly of flesh and soil says "doo" neutrally round!
- 填 (tián, tone 2): "to fill in" — See how the soil forms to fill in? It asks "Tian? Why complete?" curiously!
- 吐 (tǔ, tone 3): "to spit" — With a mouth combined with soil, you get to spit - "Too" rings out softly!
- 哇 (wā, tone 1): "Waaah!" — "Waaah!" cries the mouth happily singing "Wa!" high and loud!
- 寸 (cùn, tone 4): "Chinese Inch" — A Chinese inch hand measures, commanding "Tsun!" sharply and small!
- 封 (fēng, tone 1): "to seal" — See how the earth forms to seal? It sings "Fung!" cheerfully!
- 寺 (sì, tone 4): "Buddhist Temple" — The earth stands for buddhist temple, shouting "Sih!" sharply!
- 時 (shí, tone 2): "Time" — The sun takes the shape of time, asking "Shi? What hour?" curiously!
- 火 (huǒ, tone 3): "Fire" — The fire stands for fire, whispering "Huo" softly with flickering flames dancing high!
- 灰 (huī, tone 1): "ashes" — Like fire, this character means ashes and sings "Hway!" with flickering flames dancing high!
- 煩 (fán, tone 2): "vexed" — "Ugh, fan the flames!" she sighed, vexed and troubled by all the pages.
- 炎 (yán, tone 2): "Inflammation" — Two fires caused inflammation - "Yan, why is it so hot?" he wondered.
- 淡 (dàn, tone 4): "thin (watery/bland)" — Thin water flames yell "Dan!" sharply weakened!
- 災 (zāi, tone 1): "Disaster" — The river and fire unite to create disaster, singing "Zai!" cheerfully!
- 照 (zhào, tone 4): "to illuminate" — Like fire, this character means to illuminate and shouts "Zhao!"!
- 魚 (yú, tone 2): "a Fish" — The fire stands for a fish, asking "Yu? Why swim?" curiously!
- 漁 (yú, tone 2): "Fishing" — "Yoo-hoo, where are the fish?" the fisherman called out across the water.
- 堯 (yáo, tone 2): "Yáo" — Emperor Yao on high earth questions "Yao? How lofty?" curiously!
- 燒 (shāo, tone 1): "Fever" — The fire takes the shape of fever, singing "Shao!" cheerfully!
- 曉 (xiǎo, tone 3): "Dawn" — See how the sun forms dawn? It whispers "Shyao" softly as sunlight streams across the sky!

Task: Create a cohesive lesson narrative that weaves all 46 characters
into an epic story. Each character should appear naturally in the narrative, with its
meaning reinforced through context. Include pinyin sound cues where possible.
```

## Lesson 9 Prompt Block

```
LESSON 9 - 22 CHARACTERS

Characters to weave into narrative:
- 里 (lǐ, tone 3): "a Li" — Picture a field beside soil: that's a li, whispering "Lee" softly!
- 量 (liàng, tone 4): "quantity" — Quantity of sun under li yells "Lyang!" sharply measuring!
- 埋 (mái, tone 2): "to bury" — The soil stands for to bury, asking "Mai? Why underground?" curiously!
- 黑 (hēi, tone 1): "black" — When the fire meets the soil, they form black, calling out "Hēi!"!
- 點 (diǎn, tone 3): "Spot" — The strokes unite to show spot, whispering "Dian" softly - a vivid image to remember!
- 墨 (mò, tone 4): "Black Ink" — The soil stands for black ink, shouting "Mwoh!" sharply - a vivid image to remember!
- 冒 (mào, tone 4): "to risk" — With an eye combined with a sun, you get to risk - "Mao!" rings out sharply!
- 同 (tóng, tone 2): "same" — "Are we the same?" they questioned, standing together inside.
- 洞 (dòng, tone 4): "cave" — The water stands for cave, shouting "Dong!" sharply like ripples spreading across a pond!
- 向 (xiàng, tone 4): "orientation" — Orientation of mouth in house yells "Shyang!" sharply pointing!
- 尚 (shàng, tone 4): "to esteem" — See how the mouth forms to esteem? It shouts "Shang!" sharply!
- 字 (zì, tone 4): "character" — A character child in house yells "Zi!" sharply written!
- 守 (shǒu, tone 3): "to guard" — Picture to guard taking form - it whispers "Sho" with vivid energy!
- 完 (wán, tone 2): "to finish" — The strokes unite to show to finish, asking "Wan? Is it done?" curiously!
- 實 (shí, tone 2): "reality" — See how the roof forms reality? It asks "Shi? Is it real?" curiously!
- 宣 (xuān, tone 1): "to proclaim" — The herald proclaimed the announcement from inside the house.
- 宵 (xiāo, tone 1): "Nighttime" — At nighttime in the evening, the house was dark and quiet.
- 安 (ān, tone 1): "peaceful" — The strokes unite to show peaceful, singing "An!" cheerfully!
- 宴 (yàn, tone 4): "Banquet" — A banquet house with sun women yells "Yan!" sharply feasting!
- 寄 (jì, tone 4): "to mail" — Picture to mail taking form - it shouts "Ji!" with vivid energy!
- 富 (fù, tone 4): "wealthy" — See how the field forms wealthy? It shouts "Fu!" sharply - a vivid image to remember!
- 貯 (zhù, tone 4): "to store up" — The shellfish stands for to store up, shouting "Zhu!" sharply!

into an epic story. Each character should appear naturally in the narrative, with its

```

## Lesson 10 Prompt Block

```
LESSON 10 - 32 CHARACTERS

Characters to weave into narrative:
- 木 (mù, tone 4): "Tree" — A tree stands tall, commanding "Moo!" sharply with branches!
- 林 (lín, tone 2): "Woods" — "Lin-da, why are there so many trees?" he asked in the woods.
- 森 (sēn, tone 1): "Forest" — The dense forest had three layers of trees stacked high.
- 植 (zhí, tone 2): "to plant" — "Where should we plant the straight trees?" she asked curiously.
- 杏 (xìng, tone 4): "Apricot" — An apricot tree mouth-watering and ripe, ready for picking!
- 呆 (dāi, tone 1): "dim-witted" — A dim-witted person with wood mouth sings "Dai!" stupidly happy!
- 枯 (kū, tone 1): "withered" — With a tree combined with a wood, you get withered - "Koo!" rings out cheerfully!
- 村 (cūn, tone 1): "Village" — The strokes unite to show village, singing "Tsun!" cheerfully!
- 相 (xiāng, tone 1): "one another" — The tree and eye unite to create one another, singing "Shyang!" cheerfully!
- 本 (běn, tone 3): "notebook" — The tree takes the shape of notebook, whispering "Ben" softly!
- 案 (àn, tone 4): "legal case" — A legal case at the tree table commands "An!" sharply in judgment!
- 未 (wèi, tone 4): "not yet" — The tree takes the shape of not yet, shouting "Way!" sharply!
- 末 (mò, tone 4): "Last" — The last branch at the end of the tree was bare.
- 沫 (mò, tone 4): "Foam" — Like water, this character means foam and shouts "Mwoh!" like ripples spreading across a pond!
- 味 (wèi, tone 4): "Flavor" — See how the mouth forms flavor? It shouts "Way!" sharply spoken through parted lips!

- 曹 (cáo, tone 2): "Cao" — A striking symbol for cao that asks "TSAO?" curiously - a vivid image to remember!

into an epic story. Each character should appear naturally in the narrative, with its
meaning reinforced through context. Include pinyin sound cues where possible.
```

## Lesson 112 Prompt Block

```
LESSON 112 - 35 CHARACTERS

Characters to weave into narrative:
- 劉 (liú, tone 2): "Liu" — Picture liu taking form - it asks "LYOH?" with vivid energy!
- 潘 (pān, tone 1): "Pan" — Like water, this character means pan and sings "PAN!" like ripples spreading across a pond!
- 梁 (liáng, tone 2): "Liang" — "LYAHNG?" the water, blade, drop and tree question curiously - was Liang Qichao good or bad?
- 沈 (shěn, tone 3): "Shen" — The water takes the shape of shen, whispering "Shěn!" softly!
- 鄭 (zhèng, tone 4): "Zheng" — "JUNG!" the city walls command sharply - the surname Zheng!
- 譚 (tán, tone 2): "Tam" — "TAN?" the words question curiously - the surname Tam?
- 姚 (yáo, tone 2): "Yao" — The strokes unite to show yao, asking "YAO?" curiously - a vivid image to remember!
- 魯 (lǔ, tone 3): "Lu" — Picture lu taking form - it whispers "Lǔ!" with vivid energy!
- 姜 (jiāng, tone 1): "Jiang" — The strokes unite to show jiang, singing "JYAHNG!" cheerfully!
- 范 (fàn, tone 4): "Fan" — A striking symbol for fan that shouts "FAN!" sharply - a vivid image to remember!
- 薛 (xuē, tone 1): "Xue" — "SHWEH!" the flowers sing cheerfully - the surname Xue!
- 涂 (tú, tone 2): "Tu" — The water takes the shape of tu, asking "TOO?" curiously like ripples spreading across a pond!
- 彭 (péng, tone 2): "Peng" — The strokes unite to show peng, asking "PUNG?" curiously - a vivid image to remember!
- 郁 (yù, tone 4): "Yu" — "YOO!" the city walls command sharply - the surname Yu!
- 馮 (féng, tone 2): "Feng" — The strokes unite to show feng, asking "FUNG?" curiously - a vivid image to remember!
- 魏 (wèi, tone 4): "Wei" — Picture wei taking form - it shouts "WAY!" with vivid energy!
- 岳 (yuè, tone 4): "Yue" — Like a mountain, this character means yue and shouts "YWEH!"!
- 彿 (fú, tone 2): "as though" — This character represents as though, asking "FOO?" curiously!
- 莉 (lì, tone 4): "jasmine" — Picture jasmine taking form - it shouts "LEE!" with vivid energy!
- 湘 (xiāng, tone 1): "Hunan" — "SHYAHNG!" the water sings cheerfully through Hunan Province!
- 甸 (diàn, tone 4): "outlying areas" — "DYEN!" the field commands sharply across the outlying areas of the province!
- 滄 (cāng, tone 1): "dark blue" — "TSAHNG!" the water sings cheerfully in dark blue waves across the sea!
- 穆 (mù, tone 4): "reverent" — "MOO!" the grain commands sharply with reverent respect in the solemn ceremony!
- 娜 (ná, tone 2): "na" — "NAH?" the woman questions curiously - is her name Anna or Diana?
- 瓊 (qióng, tone 2): "fine jade" — "CHYUNG?" the jewel questions curiously - is this fine jade or green jade?
- 琳 (lín, tone 2): "gem" — "LIN?" the jewel questions curiously - a beautiful gem often used in girls' names.
- 鈞 (jūn, tone 1): "30 catties" — "JYOON!" the metal sings cheerfully - thirty catties, about 15 kg, often in boys' names!
- 喲 (yo, tone 5): "Oh" — "YOH," the mouth says neutrally - Oh! Like "yo!" between teens!
- 砲 (pào, tone 4): "cannon" — "PAO!" the stone commands sharply - a cannon firing artillery!
- 蒐 (sōu, tone 1): "search for" — "SOH!" the flowers sing cheerfully as we search for them - to seek and find!
- 芙 (fú, tone 2): "hibiscus (A)" — "FOO?" the flower questions curiously - hibiscus, the first part, like a lotus flower.
- 蓉 (róng, tone 2): "hibiscus (B)" — "RUNG?" the flower questions curiously - hibiscus, the second part, cottonrose bloom!
- Biang (biáng, tone 2): "Biang" — The heart takes the shape of biang, asking "Byahng?" curiously!
- 踐 (jiàn, tone 4): "tread on" — The leg takes the shape of tread on, shouting "Jyen!" sharply!
- 趙 (zhào, tone 4): "Zhao" — "JAO!" he commands sharply when introducing himself - the surname Zhao, like from the ancient dynasty!

Task: Create a cohesive lesson narrative that weaves all 35 characters
into an epic story. Each character should appear naturally in the narrative, with its
meaning reinforced through context. Include pinyin sound cues where possible.
```
